### Current State

**L2 barrier (confirmed DC17–DC18)**: Entity1 deadlock at r35–36 c14–18.

- Cross collection (route step 17) triggers entity1 to detach from entity2 ring and enter **tracking mode** at state 2: entity1 follows the block, maintaining a 1-row gap below block bottom, same column.
- When block descends to r35–36 c14–18 (one step above entity2), entity1 is at r37–39 c14–18. Entity1's next DOWN step would land at r42–44 c14–18 — but entity2 body (value 9, permanent) at r41–43 c15–17 blocks entity1's passage through r41. Deadlock: block cannot complete the final DOWN to r40–41 c14–18 (entity2 interior).
- Deadlock is **column-specific to c14–18**: at other columns (confirmed c29–33 post-timer-expiry in session 51), entity1 clears freely. Only the entity2 ring column is blocked.
- No alternative horizontal entry to r40–41 c14–18 exists: c9–13 void rows 35–41, c21–43 void rows 38–41. All approaches produce the same deadlock.

**What has never been tried**: Hypothesis 3A — repeatedly sending DOWN (action 1) while blocked at the deadlock. Session 51 LOCUS chose UP immediately without testing whether entity1 collision triggers a state transition. This is the single open investigation.
